`/doctor:update` for dependency-ordered cross-subsystem alignment with snapshot/validate/rollback/run log. Do not route to deleted legacy `/doctor:<name>` colon-form commands                                                                                                                                                                                |\n170: \n171: ---\n172: \n173: ## 2. ⛔ MANDATORY GATES - STOP BEFORE ACTING\n174: \n175: **⚠️ BEFORE using ANY tool (except Gate Actions: memory_match_triggers, skill_advisor.py), you MUST pass all applicable gates below.**\n176: \n177: ### 🔒 PRE-EXECUTION GATES (Pass before ANY tool use)\n178: \n179: #### GATE 1: UNDERSTANDING + CONTEXT SURFACING [SOFT] BLOCK\n180: Trigger: EACH new user message (re-evaluate even in ongoing conversations)\n181: 1. Call `memory_match_triggers(prompt)` → Surface relevant context\n182: 2. Classify intent: Research or Implementation\n183: 3. Parse request → Check confidence AND uncertainty (see §4)\n184: 4. **Dual-threshold:** confidence ≥ 0.70 AND uncertainty ≤ 0.35 → PROCEED. Either fails → INVESTIGATE (max 3 iterations) → ESCALATE. Simple: <40% ASK | 40-69% CAUTION | ≥70% PASS\n185: \n186: ####  GATE 2: SKILL ROUTING [REQUIRED for non-trivial tasks]\n187: 1. A) Primary: use the automatic Skill Advisor Hook brief already surfaced by the runtime when present. See `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/references/hooks/skill-advisor-hook.md`.\n188: 2. B) Fallback: run `python3 .opencode/skills/system-skill-advisor/mcp_server/scripts/skill_advisor.py \"[request]\" --threshold 0.8` when no hook brief is present, when scripting a check, or when diagnosing hook behavior.\n189: 3. C) Cite user's explicit direction: \"User specified: [exact quote]\"\n190: - Confidence ≥ 0.8 → MUST invoke skill | < 0.8 → general approach | User names skill → cite and proceed\n191: - Output: `SKILL ROUTING: [result]` or `SKILL ROUTING: User directed → [name]`\n192: - Skip: trivial queries only (greetings, single-line questions)\n193: \n194: #### GATE 3: SPEC FOLDER QUESTION [HARD] BLOCK - PRIORITY GATE\n195: - **Overrides Gates 1-2:** If file modification detected → ask Gate 3 BEFORE any analysis/tool calls\n196: - **Machine contract:** `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/shared/gate-3-classifier.ts` (`classifyPrompt()`). The prose lists below are human-readable; the classifier module is authoritative for runtimes that call it.\n197: - **Positive triggers (write actions):** create, add, remove, delete, rename, move, update, change, modify, edit, fix, refactor, implement, build, write, generate, configure\n198: - **Positive triggers (continuity writes):** `save context`, `save memory`, `/memory:save`, `/speckit:resume`, `resume iteration`, `resume deep research`, `resume deep review`, `continue iteration` (these produce `description.json` / `graph-metadata.json` / continuity frontmatter / `iteration-NNN.md` writes)\n199: - **Read-only disqualifiers:** `review`, `audit`, `inspect`, `analyze`, `explain` — suppress Gate 3 when they appear ALONE (e.g. \"review the decomposition phase\"). Do NOT suppress when a continuity-write trigger is also present.\n200: - **Note:** tokens `analyze`, `decompose`, `phase` are NOT positive triggers; they false-positive on read-only review prompts.\n201: - **Options:** A) Existing | B) New | C) Update related | D) Skip | E) Phase folder (e.g., `specs/NNN-name/001-phase/`)\n202: - **Router commands:** For router-style commands such as `/doctor`, evaluate Gate 3 per selected route. The route manifest/table must expose each target's location and mutation class (`read-only`, `add-only`, `mutates`) before asking or acting.\n203: - **Ask first, then act.** No Read/Edit/Write/Bash (except Gate Actions) before answer. The answer applies for the ENTIRE session — re-ask ONLY when user says \"new task\" / \"different feature\" / names a different spec folder, or asks you to re-ask.\n204: \n205: Router command manifests must make the mutation boundary visible before execution:\n206: - `read-only` routes may inspect and report without a spec-folder write path.\n207: - `add-only` routes may create scoped logs, snapshots, or evidence after Gate 3 is satisfied.\n208: - `mutates` routes require the same spec-folder discipline as any other file/database mutation.\n209: \n210: #### GATE 4: SKILL-OWNED WORKFLOW TIEBREAKERS\n211: Trigger-phrase routing (\"deep-research\", \"deep-review\", \":auto\", \"iterations\", \"convergence\") and state-machine discipline (no manual `/tmp` state, no direct `@deep-research` / `@deep-review` Task dispatch, no skipping `deep-research-state.jsonl` / `deltas/` / `logs/`) are enforced by Gate 2 (Skill Advisor at ≥ 0.8) plus the `/deep:start-research-loop` and `/deep:start-review-loop` skill SKILL.md invariants. The two tiebreakers below are NOT covered there:\n212: - **Executor CLI ≠ skill route.** \"Use cli-codex gpt-5.5 high\" is the HOW — it still runs INSIDE the skill's workflow. Never let the executor name override the skill-owned route.\n213: - **Skill advisor ambiguity.** When `command-spec-kit` matches alongside `cli-*` for iteration phrases, `command-spec-kit` wins. The CLI executor is a tool inside the command's workflow, not a replacement for it.\n214: \n215: #### CONSOLIDATED QUESTION PROTOCOL\n216: Consolidate multiple questions into a SINGLE prompt before any analysis or tool calls — never split across messages. **Bypass phrases:** \"skip context\" / \"fresh start\" / \"skip memory\" / [skip] for memory loading; Level 1 tasks skip completion verification.\n217: \n218: ---\n219: \n220: ### 🔒 POST-EXECUTION GATES\n221: \n222: #### MEMORY SAVE RULE [HARD] BLOCK\n223: Trigger: \"save context\", \"save memory\", `/memory:save`\n224: - If spec folder established at Gate 3 → USE IT (don't re-ask). Carry-over applies ONLY to memory saves\n225: - If NO folder and Gate 3 never answered → HARD BLOCK → Ask user\n226: - **Full save (DB + embeddings + graph):** `node .opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/scripts/dist/memory/generate-context.js`\n227:   - AI composes structured JSON with session context, writes to `/tmp/save-context-data.json`, passes as first arg. Alternatively use `--json '<inline-json>'` or `--stdin`.\n228:   - Also refreshes `graph-metadata.json` and `description.json` for the spec folder.\n229: - **Quick continuity update:** AI may directly edit `_memory.continuity` YAML frontmatter blocks in `implementation-summary.md` without running generate-context.js (per ADR-004). The resume ladder only reads continuity from `implementation-summary.md`.\n230: - **Memory mutation freshness:** Handlers that affect `memory_index` rows (`memory_save`, `memory_bulk_delete`) must invalidate the entity-density cache after commit so graph-channel routing sees fresh causal/entity state without waiting for the TTL.\n231: - **Indexing:** For immediate MCP visibility after save: `memory_index_scan({ specFolder })` or `memory_save()`\n232: - **Post-Save Review:** After `generate-context.js` completes, check the POST-SAVE QUALITY REVIEW output.\n233:   - **HIGH** issues: MUST manually patch via Edit tool (fix title, trigger_phrases, importance_tier)\n234:   - **MEDIUM** issues: patch when practical\n235:   - **PASSED/SKIPPED**: no action needed\n236: \n237: #### COMPLETION VERIFICATION RULE [HARD] BLOCK\n238: Trigger: Claiming \"done\", \"complete\", \"finished\", \"works\"\n239: 1. Run `bash .opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/scripts/spec/validate.sh <spec-folder> --strict` (Exit 0 = pass, 1 = warnings, 2 = errors).\n240: 2. Load `checklist.md` → verify ALL items → mark `[x]` with evidence.\n241: 3. Reconcile completion metadata: update `spec.md` Status, plan/checklist evidence, handover completion fields, and implementation-summary continuity so packet docs do not claim conflicting completion states.\n242: - Skip: Level 1 tasks (no checklist.md required).\n243: \n244: Completion metadata reconciliation covers:\n245: - `spec.md` status and shipped/current-state claims.\n246: - `plan.md` / `tasks.md` / `checklist.md` evidence rows.\n247: - `handover.md` or `_memory.continuity` fields when present.\n248: - `implementation-summary.md` final state, validation evidence, and continuation notes.\n249: \n250: #### VIOLATION RECOVERY [SELF-CORRECTION]\n251: Trigger: About to skip gates, or realized gates were skipped → STOP → STATE: \"Before I proceed, I need to ask about documentation:\" → ASK Gate 3 (A/B/C/D/E) → WAIT\n252: - **Exception:** If the user already answered Gate 3 earlier in this conversation for the same task, do NOT re-ask. Reuse the existing answer and proceed.\n253: \n254: #### Self-Check (before ANY tool-using response):\n255: - [ ] File modification? Asked spec folder question?\n256: - [ ] Skill routing verified?\n257: - [ ] Saving memory? Using `generate-context.js` (not Write tool)?\n258: - [ ] Aligned with ORIGINAL request? No scope drift?\n259: - [ ] Claiming completion? `checklist.md` verified?\n260: \n261: ---\n262: \n263: ## 3. 📝 SPEC FOLDER DOCUMENTATION\n264: \n265: Every conversation that modifies files MUST have a spec folder. **Full details:** system-spec-kit SKILL.md (§1 When to Use, §3 How it Works, §4 Rules)\n266: \n267: ### Documentation Levels\n268: \n269: | Level            | LOC                     | Required Files                                                         | Use When                                                                                          |\n270: | ---------------- | ----------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |\n271: | **1**            | <100                    | spec.md, plan.md, tasks.md, implementation-summary.md                  | All features (minimum)                                                                            |\n272: | **2**            | 100-499                 | Level 1 + checklist.md                                                 | QA validation needed                                                                              |\n273: | **3**            | ≥500                    | Level 2 + decision-record.md (+ optional research.md, resource-map.md) | Complex/architecture changes                                                                      |\n274: | **3+**           | Complexity 80+          | Level 3 + AI protocols, extended checklist, sign-offs                  | Multi-agent, enterprise governance                                                                |\n275: | **Phase Parent** | n/a (control file only) | spec.md, description.json, graph-metadata.json                         | Folder contains phase children (`[0-9]{3}-name/` subdirs with their own spec.md/description.json) |\n276: \n277: **Optional cross-cutting docs (any level)**: `handover.md`, `debug-delegation.md`, `research.md`, and `resource-map.md` - copy from `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/templates/` as needed. For phase parents that have undergone reorganization (renames, gap renumbering, consolidation), `context-index.md` provides a migration bridge — optional, no required template.\n278: \n279: **Phase Parent Mode:** When a spec folder contains at least one direct child matching `^[0-9]{3}-[a-z0-9-]+$` AND that child has `spec.md` OR `description.json`, the validator treats the folder as a phase parent and ONLY requires `{spec.md, description.json, graph-metadata.json}` at the parent level. Heavy docs (`plan.md`, `tasks.md`, `checklist.md`, `decision-record.md`, `implementation-summary.md`) live in the phase children where they stay accurate to that phase's actual work. Detection rule: `is_phase_parent()` (shell) and `isPhaseParent()` (TS/JS) are the single source of truth — both must agree. **Content discipline:** the phase-parent `spec.md` must NOT narrate consolidation, merge, or migration history — it documents root purpose, sub-phase control file, and what needs done. Migration history goes in `context-index.md` if needed. Resume on a phase parent first follows a fresh `derived.last_active_child_id` pointer from `graph-metadata.json`; missing, null, stale, or `--no-redirect` cases list child phases with statuses (per `/speckit:resume` step 3b) so the user can pick which phase to continue. Tolerant policy: legacy phase parents that retain heavy docs continue to validate; soft-deprecation is a follow-on packet.\n280: \n281: **Mandatory metadata:** Every spec folder (Level 1+) MUST contain `description.json` and `graph-metadata.json`. Both are auto-generated/refreshed by `generate-context.js` during canonical saves. `graph-metadata.json` stores lowercase derived status and falls back to `implementation-summary.md` presence plus checklist completion when explicit status is absent. If creating a spec folder manually or via template, run `generate-description.js` and the graph-metadata backfill to ensure both files exist. Spec folders without these files are invisible to memory search and graph traversal.\n282: \n283: **Rules:** When in doubt → higher level. LOC is soft guidance (risk/complexity can override). Single typo/whitespace fixes (<5 characters in one file) are exempt.\n284: \n285: **Spec folder path:** `.opencode/specs/[track]/[###-short-name]/` for tracked OpenCode packets, with phase children such as `[001-phase]/` under phase parents. Legacy/root `specs/[###-short-name]/` may exist, but current packet-local docs and metadata live under `.opencode/specs/`. | **Templates:** `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/templates/`\n286: \n287: ---\n288: \n289: ## 4. 🧑‍🏫 CONFIDENCE & CLARIFICATION FRAMEWORK\n290: \n291: #### Confidence Thresholds\n292: \n293: | Confidence   | Action                                       |\n294: | ------------ | -------------------------------------------- |\n295: | **≥80%**     | Proceed with citable source                  |\n296: | **40-79%**   | Proceed with caveats                         |\n297: | **<40%**     | Ask for clarification or mark \"UNKNOWN\"      |\n298: | **Override** | Blockers/conflicts → ask regardless of score |\n299: \n300: #### Logic-Sync Protocol\n301: \n302: On contradiction (Spec vs Code, conflicting requirements) → HALT → Report \"LOGIC-SYNC REQUIRED: [Fact A] contradicts [Fact B]\" → Ask \"Which truth prevails?\"\n303: \n304: #### Escalation\n305: \n306: Confidence stays <80% after two failed attempts → ask with 2-3 options. Blockers beyond control → escalate with evidence and proposed next step.\n307: \n308: ---\n309: \n310: ## 5. 🤖 AGENT ROUTING\n311: \n312: When using the orchestrate agent or Task tool for complex multi-step workflows, route to specialized agents:\n313: \n314: ### Runtime Agent Directory Resolution\n315: \n316: Use the agent directory that matches the active runtime/provider profile:\n317: \n318: | Runtime / Profile | Agent Directory     |\n319: | ----------------- | ------------------- |\n320: | **Opencode**      | `.opencode/agents/` |\n321: | **Claude Code**   | `.claude/agents/`   |\n322: | **Codex CLI**     | `.codex/agents/`    |\n323: | **Gemini CLI**    | `.gemini/agents/`   |\n324: \n325: **Resolution rule:** pick one directory by runtime and stay consistent for that workflow phase.\n326: \n327: ### Agent Definitions\n328: \n329: - **`@orchestrate`** - Multi-agent coordination, complex workflows\n330: - **`@code`** - Application-code implementation specialist (LEAF, write-capable). Stack-aware via `sk-code` skill delegation; fail-closed verification. Dispatched ONLY by `@orchestrate` (orchestrator-only convention).\n331: - **`@context`** - LEAF-only retrieval agent for codebase search, pattern discovery, and context loading. Uses memory triggers/context, memory search, CocoIndex, and direct code evidence. LEAF: no sub-agent dispatch, no Task tool, no writes.\n332: - **`@review`** - Code review, PRs, quality gates (READ-ONLY)\n333: - **`@debug`** - Fresh perspective debugging (5-phase root-cause). Dispatched via Task tool; retains exclusive write access for `debug-delegation.md`\n334: - **`@markdown`** - Template-first markdown/documentation executor (LEAF, write-capable). Handles `/create:*` commands, orchestrator-scoped spec-doc authoring, and any explicitly scoped markdown writing task with a resolved output path. Loads `sk-doc` on every invocation, reads the command-mapped or document-appropriate template before writing, and refuses only unscoped writes, path-ambiguous targets, or nested delegation. The Phase 0 gate is scope-based, not `/create:*`-only. Gate 3 still applies to writes unless the user or command contract has already supplied the answer.\n335: - **`@prompt-improver`** - Prompt engineering via `sk-prompt`. Dispatched by `/improve:prompt`\n336: - **`@ai-council`** - Deep AI Council planning architect for multi-seat deliberation, strategy comparison, critique, convergence, and packet-local `ai-council/**` artifacts.\n337: - **`@deep-research`** - Autonomous deep research iterations (LEAF). Dispatched by `/deep:start-research-loop`\n338: - **`@deep-review`** - Autonomous deep review iterations (LEAF, P0/P1/P2). Dispatched by `/deep:start-review-loop`\n339: - **`@deep-agent-improvement`** - Bounded agent improvement via `deep-agent-improvement`. Dispatched by `/improve:agent`\n340: \n341: #### Distributed Governance Rule\n342: \n343: - **Template + strict validate:** Any agent writing authored spec-folder docs (`spec.md`, `plan.md`, `tasks.md`, `checklist.md`, `implementation-summary.md`, `decision-record.md`, `handover.md`, `review-report.md`, `debug-delegation.md`, `resource-map.md`) MUST use templates from `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/templates/` and run `bash .opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/scripts/spec/validate.sh <spec-folder> --strict` after the write, before any completion claim.\n344: - **Continuity updates:** route through `/memory:save`.\n345: - **Deep-research exemption:** workflow-owned packet markdown (`research/iterations/*.md`, `research/deep-research-*.md`, progressive `research/research.md` updates) is exempt from the per-write strict-validate rule; `/deep:start-research-loop` instead runs targeted strict validation after every `spec.md` mutation it performs.\n346: - **Exclusive write access:** `@deep-research` owns `research/research.md`; `@debug` owns `debug-delegation.md`.\n347: \n348: ---\n349: \n350: ## 6. ⚙️  MCP TOOL ROUTING\n351: \n352: **Two systems:**\n353: \n354: 1. **Native MCP** (`opencode.json`) - Direct tools, called natively. **6 servers registered:**\n355:    - Sequential Thinking\n356:    - Spec Kit Memory (`mk-spec-memory`, 39 tools)\n357:    - Skill Advisor (`mk_skill_advisor`, 9 tools — 8 public + 1 internal)\n358:    - Code Graph (`mk_code_index`, 11 tools)\n359:    - CocoIndex Code\n360:    - Code Mode\n361: \n362: 2. **Code Mode MCP** (`.utcp_config.json`) - External tools via `call_tool_chain()`\n363:    - Figma, Github, ClickUp, Chrome DevTools, etc.\n364:    - Naming: `{manual_name}.{manual_name}_{tool_name}` (e.g., `clickup.clickup_get_teams({})`)\n365:    - Discovery: `search_tools()`, `list_tools()`, or read `.utcp_config.json`\n366:   \n367: ---\n368: \n369: ## 7. 🧩 SKILL ROUTING REFERENCE\n370: \n371: Skills are specialized, on-demand support that provide domain expertise. Unlike knowledge files (passive references), skills are explicitly invoked to handle complex, multi-step workflows.\n372: \n373: ### How Skills Work\n374: \n375: ```\n376: Task Received → Gate 2: Read hook brief, or run skill_advisor.py fallback\n377:                     ↓\n378:     Confidence > 0.8 → MUST invoke recommended skill\n379:                     ↓\n380:      Invoke Skill → Read(\".opencode/skills/<skill-name>/SKILL.md\")\n381:                     ↓\n382:     Instructions Load → SKILL.md content + resource paths\n383:                     ↓\n384:       Follow Instructions → Complete task using skill guidance\n385: ```\n386: \n387: ### Skill Loading Protocol\n388: \n389: 1. Gate 2 provides skill recommendation via the Skill Advisor Hook, or via `skill_advisor.py` when the hook is unavailable.\n390: 2. Invoke using appropriate method for your environment\n391: 3. Read bundled resources from `references/`, `scripts/`, `assets/` paths\n392: 4. Follow skill instructions to completion\n393: 5. Do NOT re-invoke a skill already in context\n\n(End of file - total 393 lines)\n</content>","metadata":{"preview":"# AI Assistant Framework (Universal Template)\n\n> **Universal behavior framework** defining guardrails, standards, and decision protocols.\n\n---\n\n### Multi-Repository Architecture\n\n**Universal Framework:** Code work behavior is handled automatically by the `sk-code` skill, which routes between code surfaces detected at dispatch time. The active set of detection markers and per-surface patterns lives inside `sk-code` — see `.opencode/skills/sk-code/SKILL.md` §2 Smart Routing for the current detection list and `references/<surface>/` for per-surface conventions.\n\n**How It Works:** `sk-code` detects the active code surface from CWD/target paths and library markers, loads patterns from `.opencode/skills/sk-code/references/<surface>/`, and selects surface-appropriate verification (see Quick Reference). Surfaces it does not recognize trigger a disambiguation question rather than guessing.\n12: \n13: **The Iron Law:** NO completion claims without running stack-appropriate verification.\n14: \n15: ---\n16: \n17: ## 1. 🚨 CRITICAL RULES\n18: \n19: ### Safety Constraints\n20: \n21: **HARD BLOCKERS (The \"Four Laws\" of Agent Safety):**\n22: 1. **READ FIRST:** Never edit a file without reading it first. Understand context before modifying.\n23: 2. **SCOPE LOCK:** Only modify files explicitly in scope. **NO** \"cleaning up\" or \"improving\" adjacent code. Scope in `spec.md` is FROZEN.\n24: 3. **VERIFY:** Syntax checks and tests **MUST** pass before claiming completion. **NO** blind commits.\n25: 4. **HALT:** Stop immediately if uncertain, if line numbers don't match, or if tests fail.\n26: \n27: **HALT CONDITIONS (Stop and Report):**\n28: - [ ] Target file does not exist or line numbers don't match.\n29: - [ ] Syntax check or Tests fail after edit.\n30: - [ ] Merge conflicts encountered.\n31: - [ ] Edit tool reports \"string not found\".\n32: - [ ] Test/Production boundary is unclear.\n33: \n34: **OPERATIONAL MANDATES:**\n35: - **All file modifications require a spec folder** (Gate 3).\n36: - **Never lie or fabricate** - use \"UNKNOWN\" when uncertain.\n37: - **Clarify** if confidence < 80% (see §4 Confidence Framework).\n38: - **Use explicit uncertainty:** Prefix claims with \"I'M UNCERTAIN ABOUT THIS:\".\n39: - **CLI dispatch rule** — Before composing any prompt for `cli-X` (devin / codex / claude-code / gemini / opencode), you MUST `Read` `.opencode/skills/cli-X/SKILL.md` first. Advisor confidence ≥ 0.8 does NOT waive this. Skills carry model-specific prompt-quality contracts (e.g. SWE-1.6's RCAF + medium-density pre-planning rule) that are not in the binary's `--help` and easy to miss. Any `<binary> --model <X>` invocation for a CLI with a `cli-X` skill requires the skill file in context.\n40: - **Small-model dispatch rule** — Before dispatching to small models (SWE-1.6, DeepSeek-v4-pro, Kimi-k2.6, Qwen3.6, GLM-5.1 via cli-devin and/or cli-opencode; optional Haiku/Gemini Flash), you MUST consult `sk-ai-small-model` for pointers to context-budget defaults, output-verification recipes, model-profile registry, and structured-permissions schema. The sentinel skill is the single discoverable home for small-model optimization patterns and the canonical dispatch matrix (executor + provider + quota_pool per model). Routing is automatic via the advisor's `enhances` edges from cli-devin and cli-opencode, but the rule is here for explicit verification when sk-ai-small-model doesn't auto-surface.\n41: \n42: ---\n43: \n44: ### Request Analysis & Execution\n45: \n46: **Flow:** Parse request → Read files first → Analyze → Design simplest solution → Validate → Execute\n47: \n48: #### Execution Behavior\n49: \n50: - **Plan before acting** on multi-step work. Decide which files to read first, which tools to use, and how the result will be verified before making changes.\n51: - **Use a research-first approach.** Read the actual code, docs, and local instructions first. Never use an edit-first approach, and prefer surgical edits over broad rewrites.\n52: - **Apply project-specific conventions from `AGENTS.md`** before acting.\n53: - **Take responsibility for issues encountered during execution.** Do not dodge ownership with phrases like `not caused by my changes` or `pre-existing issue`; work toward the fix.\n54: - **Do not stop early when the requested solution is still incomplete.** Do not frame partial progress as a `good stopping point`, `natural checkpoint`, or `future work` when a safe path forward exists.\n55: - **Do not ask for permission to continue when the next safe step is already clear and in scope.** Avoid `should I continue?` or `want me to keep going?` when you can proceed safely under the existing rules.\n56: - **Use frequent self-checks and reasoning loops** to catch and fix your own mistakes before asking for help.\n57: - **Reason from actual data, not assumptions.** Verify against the real files, outputs, and behavior in front of you.\n58: \n59: \n60: ---\n61: \n62: ### Required Tools & Search Routing\n63: \n64: **MANDATORY TOOLS:**\n65: - **Spec Kit Memory MCP** - research, context recovery, saves. See Memory Save Rule below for save mechanics.\n66: - **CocoIndex Code MCP** - semantic code search. MUST use when exploring unfamiliar code, finding implementations by concept/intent, or when Grep/Glob exact matching is insufficient. Skill: `.opencode/skills/mcp-coco-index/`\n67: - **Git (sk-git)** - worktree setup, conventional commits, PR creation. Full details: `.opencode/skills/sk-git/`. Trigger keywords: worktree, branch, commit, merge, pr, pull request, git workflow, finish work, integrate changes\n68: \n69: **CODE SEARCH DECISION TREE:**\n70: \n71: ```text\n72: Need to find code?\n73:   |\n74:   +-- Know the exact text/token/symbol?\n75:   |     YES --> Grep (exact match)\n76:   |\n77:   +-- Know the file name or path?\n78:   |     YES --> Glob (pattern match)\n79:   |\n80:   +-- Searching by concept, intent, or \"how does X work\"?\n81:   |     YES --> CocoIndex search (semantic)\n82:   |             +-- Verify hits with Read\n83:   |             +-- Confirm with Grep if needed\n84:   |\n85:   +-- Exploring unfamiliar code?\n86:         YES --> CocoIndex search FIRST, then Grep/Glob to fill gaps\n87: ```\n88: \n89: CocoIndex triggers: \"find code that does X\", \"how is X implemented\", \"where is the logic for X\", \"similar code\", \"find patterns\", exploring unfamiliar modules, any intent-based query where exact tokens are unknown.\n90: \n91: | Approach     | Command                                                       | When                 |\n92: | ------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------- |\n93: | **MCP tool** | `search(query, languages, paths, num_results, refresh_index)` | AI agent integration |\n94: | **CLI**      | `ccc search \"query\" --lang X --path Y --limit N`              | Direct terminal use  |\n95: \n96: Set `refresh_index=false` after the first search in a session unless the codebase changed.\n97: \n98: ---\n99: \n100: ### Startup & Resume Recovery\n101: \n102: Hook-capable runtimes (Claude, Codex, Gemini, OpenCode) may inject startup context when wired. Per-runtime triggers: `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/references/config/hook_system.md`. Feature-flag defaults: `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/ENV_REFERENCE.md` (\"Feature flags reference table\").\n103: \n104: **Recovery flow when hooks are unavailable or fail:**\n105: \n106: 1. `/speckit:resume` is the canonical surface; rebuild context in order: `handover.md` → `_memory.continuity` → canonical spec docs (`implementation-summary.md` → `tasks.md` → `plan.md` → `spec.md`).\n107: 2. **Phase parent** (target has `[0-9]{3}-name/` children with their own spec/description): honor `graph-metadata.json.derived.last_active_child_id`, else list children with statuses. Lean trio policy — only `spec.md`, `description.json`, `graph-metadata.json` live at parent; read the chosen child's continuity ladder, NOT the parent's plan/tasks/implementation-summary.\n108: 3. Stale or missing structural context: run `session_bootstrap()`, then `code_graph_scan` if needed. Graph unavailable: use CocoIndex + direct reads, but keep the packet-local continuity ladder as source-of-truth. Code-graph implementation/docs are owned by `.opencode/skills/system-code-graph/`; tool names stay stable.\n109: 4. Re-anchor on spec folder, current task, blockers, and next steps before making changes.\n110: \n111: ---\n112: \n113: ### Quality & Anti-Patterns\n114: \n115: **QUALITY PRINCIPLES:**\n116: - **Prefer simplicity**, reuse existing patterns, and cite evidence with sources\n117: - Solve only the stated problem; **avoid over-engineering** and premature optimization\n118: - **Verify with checks** (simplicity, performance, maintainability, scope) before making changes\n119: - **Truth over agreement** - correct user misconceptions with evidence; do not agree for conversational flow\n120: \n121: **ANTI-PATTERNS (Detect Silently):**\n122: \n123: | Anti-Pattern           | Trigger Phrases                                 | Response                                                                    |\n124: | ---------------------- | ----------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------- |\n125: | Over-engineering       | \"for flexibility\", \"future-proof\", \"might need\" | Ask: \"Is this solving a current problem or a hypothetical one?\"             |\n126: | Premature optimization | \"could be slow\", \"might bottleneck\"             | Ask: \"Has this been measured? What's the actual performance?\"               |\n127: | Cargo culting          | \"best practice\", \"always should\"                | Ask: \"Does this pattern fit this specific case?\"                            |\n128: | Gold-plating           | \"while we're here\", \"might as well\"             | Flag scope creep: \"That's a separate change - shall I note it for later?\"   |\n129: | Wrong abstraction      | \"DRY this up\" for 2 instances                   | \"These look similar but might not be the same concept. Let's verify first.\" |\n130: | Scope creep            | \"also add\", \"bonus feature\"                     | \"That's outside the current scope. Want to track it separately?\"            |\n131: \n132: **ANALYSIS LENSES:**\n133: \n134: | Lens               | Focus            | Detection Questions                                                                |\n135: | ------------------ | ---------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |\n136: | **CLARITY**        | Simplicity       | Is this the simplest code that solves the problem? Are abstractions earned?        |\n137: | **SYSTEMS**        | Dependencies     | What does this change touch? What calls this? What are the side effects?           |\n138: | **BIAS**           | Wrong problem    | Is user solving a symptom? Is this premature optimization? Is the framing correct? |\n139: | **SUSTAINABILITY** | Maintainability  | Will future devs understand this? Is it self-documenting? Tech debt implications?  |\n140: | **VALUE**          | Actual impact    | Does this change behavior or just refactor? Is it cosmetic or functional?          |\n141: | **SCOPE**          | Complexity match | Does solution complexity match problem size? Single-line fix or new abstraction?   |\n142: \n143: ---\n144: \n145: ### Quick Reference: Common Workflows\n146: \n147: | Task                                 | Flow                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |\n148: | ------------------------------------ | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |\n149: | **Resume prior work**                | `/speckit:resume` → Rebuild context from `handover.md` → `_memory.continuity` → canonical spec docs → Review → Continue                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |\n150: | **New spec folder**                  | Option B (Gate 3) → Research via Task tool → Evidence-based plan → Approval → Implement                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |\n151: | **Code work**                        | sk-code skill → smart router (auto-detects the active stack from CWD + library markers; unsupported surfaces ask for disambiguation); Phase 1-3 (Implement → Quality Gate → Debug → Verify)                                                                                                                                                                |\n152: | **File modification**                | Gate 3 (ask spec folder) → Gate 1 → Gate 2 → Load memory context → Execute                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |\n153: | **Code search**                      | CocoIndex for semantic/intent → Grep for exact text → Glob for file paths → Read for contents                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |\n154: | **Research/exploration**             | `memory_match_triggers()` → `memory_context()` (unified) OR `memory_search()` (targeted) → Document findings                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |\n155: | **Git workflow**                     | sk-git skill → Worktree setup / Commit / Finish (PR)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |\n156: | **Prompt improvement**    | Prompt engineering via `sk-prompt`. Dispatched by `/improve:prompt`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |\n157: | **Markdown writing** | `@markdown` → general markdown/spec writing OR `/create:*` commands → `sk-doc` template → write artifact |\n158: | **Documentation quality** | `sk-doc` skill → classify → template → validate → DQI score → verify |\n159: | **Phase workflow**                   | `/speckit:plan :with-phases` or `/speckit:complete :with-phases` → Decompose → Populate → Plan first child                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |\n160: | **Deep research**                    | `/deep:start-research-loop` → Init → Loop iterations → Convergence → Synthesize → Memory save                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |\n161: | **Deep review**                      | `/deep:start-review-loop` → Scope → Loop iterations → Convergence → review-report.md → Memory save                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |\n162: | **Deep AI Council**                  | `@ai-council` → Seats deliberate → Critique → Converge → `ai-council/**` artifacts → Council test gate                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |\n163: | **Claim completion**                 | Run `bash .opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/scripts/spec/validate.sh <spec-folder> --strict` → Load `checklist.md` → Verify ALL items → Mark with evidence                                                                                                                                                                                                  |\n164: | **Save context**                     | `/memory:save` OR compose JSON → `generate-context.js --json '<data>' [spec-folder]` → Auto-indexed                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |\n165: | **End session**                      | `/memory:save` → `handover_state` routing updates `handover.md` → Provide continuation prompt                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |\n166: | **Memory DB admin**                  | `/memory:manage` → stats, health, cleanup, retention, validate, checkpoint, ingest, CCC operations                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |\n167: | **Analysis/evaluation**              | `/memory:search` → preflight, postflight, causal graph, ablation, dashboard, history; inspect `memory_health.data.routing` for graph/degree channel utilization                                                                                                                                                                                            |\n168: | **Constitutional memory**            | `/memory:learn` → create, list, edit, remove, budget                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |\n169: | **Doctor command surface**           | `/doctor <target>` argv-positional router for subsystem diagnostics/repairs (memory, causal-graph, code-graph, deep-loop, cocoindex, skill-advisor, skill-budget); `/doctor:mcp install\\|debug` for MCP infra; `/doctor:update` for dependency-ordered cross-subsystem alignment with snapshot/validate/rollback/run log. Do not route to deleted legacy `/doctor:<name>` colon-form commands                                                                                                                                                                                |\n170: \n171: ---\n172: \n173: ## 2. ⛔ MANDATORY GATES - STOP BEFORE ACTING\n174: \n175: **⚠️ BEFORE using ANY tool (except Gate Actions: memory_match_triggers, skill_advisor.py), you MUST pass all applicable gates below.**\n176: \n177: ### 🔒 PRE-EXECUTION GATES (Pass before ANY tool use)\n178: \n179: #### GATE 1: UNDERSTANDING + CONTEXT SURFACING [SOFT] BLOCK\n180: Trigger: EACH new user message (re-evaluate even in ongoing conversations)\n181: 1. Call `memory_match_triggers(prompt)` → Surface relevant context\n182: 2. Classify intent: Research or Implementation\n183: 3. Parse request → Check confidence AND uncertainty (see §4)\n184: 4. **Dual-threshold:** confidence ≥ 0.70 AND uncertainty ≤ 0.35 → PROCEED. Either fails → INVESTIGATE (max 3 iterations) → ESCALATE. Simple: <40% ASK | 40-69% CAUTION | ≥70% PASS\n185: \n186: ####  GATE 2: SKILL ROUTING [REQUIRED for non-trivial tasks]\n187: 1. A) Primary: use the automatic Skill Advisor Hook brief already surfaced by the runtime when present. See `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/references/hooks/skill-advisor-hook.md`.\n188: 2. B) Fallback: run `python3 .opencode/skills/system-skill-advisor/mcp_server/scripts/skill_advisor.py \"[request]\" --threshold 0.8` when no hook brief is present, when scripting a check, or when diagnosing hook behavior.\n189: 3. C) Cite user's explicit direction: \"User specified: [exact quote]\"\n190: - Confidence ≥ 0.8 → MUST invoke skill | < 0.8 → general approach | User names skill → cite and proceed\n191: - Output: `SKILL ROUTING: [result]` or `SKILL ROUTING: User directed → [name]`\n192: - Skip: trivial queries only (greetings, single-line questions)\n193: \n194: #### GATE 3: SPEC FOLDER QUESTION [HARD] BLOCK - PRIORITY GATE\n195: - **Overrides Gates 1-2:** If file modification detected → ask Gate 3 BEFORE any analysis/tool calls\n196: - **Machine contract:** `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/shared/gate-3-classifier.ts` (`classifyPrompt()`). The prose lists below are human-readable; the classifier module is authoritative for runtimes that call it.\n197: - **Positive triggers (write actions):** create, add, remove, delete, rename, move, update, change, modify, edit, fix, refactor, implement, build, write, generate, configure\n198: - **Positive triggers (continuity writes):** `save context`, `save memory`, `/memory:save`, `/speckit:resume`, `resume iteration`, `resume deep research`, `resume deep review`, `continue iteration` (these produce `description.json` / `graph-metadata.json` / continuity frontmatter / `iteration-NNN.md` writes)\n199: - **Read-only disqualifiers:** `review`, `audit`, `inspect`, `analyze`, `explain` — suppress Gate 3 when they appear ALONE (e.g. \"review the decomposition phase\"). Do NOT suppress when a continuity-write trigger is also present.\n200: - **Note:** tokens `analyze`, `decompose`, `phase` are NOT positive triggers; they false-positive on read-only review prompts.\n201: - **Options:** A) Existing | B) New | C) Update related | D) Skip | E) Phase folder (e.g., `specs/NNN-name/001-phase/`)\n202: - **Router commands:** For router-style commands such as `/doctor`, evaluate Gate 3 per selected route. The route manifest/table must expose each target's location and mutation class (`read-only`, `add-only`, `mutates`) before asking or acting.\n203: - **Ask first, then act.** No Read/Edit/Write/Bash (except Gate Actions) before answer. The answer applies for the ENTIRE session — re-ask ONLY when user says \"new task\" / \"different feature\" / names a different spec folder, or asks you to re-ask.\n204: \n205: Router command manifests must make the mutation boundary visible before execution:\n206: - `read-only` routes may inspect and report without a spec-folder write path.\n207: - `add-only` routes may create scoped logs, snapshots, or evidence after Gate 3 is satisfied.\n208: - `mutates` routes require the same spec-folder discipline as any other file/database mutation.\n209: \n210: #### GATE 4: SKILL-OWNED WORKFLOW TIEBREAKERS\n211: Trigger-phrase routing (\"deep-research\", \"deep-review\", \":auto\", \"iterations\", \"convergence\") and state-machine discipline (no manual `/tmp` state, no direct `@deep-research` / `@deep-review` Task dispatch, no skipping `deep-research-state.jsonl` / `deltas/` / `logs/`) are enforced by Gate 2 (Skill Advisor at ≥ 0.8) plus the `/deep:start-research-loop` and `/deep:start-review-loop` skill SKILL.md invariants. The two tiebreakers below are NOT covered there:\n212: - **Executor CLI ≠ skill route.** \"Use cli-codex gpt-5.5 high\" is the HOW — it still runs INSIDE the skill's workflow. Never let the executor name override the skill-owned route.\n213: - **Skill advisor ambiguity.** When `command-spec-kit` matches alongside `cli-*` for iteration phrases, `command-spec-kit` wins. The CLI executor is a tool inside the command's workflow, not a replacement for it.\n214: \n215: #### CONSOLIDATED QUESTION PROTOCOL\n216: Consolidate multiple questions into a SINGLE prompt before any analysis or tool calls — never split across messages. **Bypass phrases:** \"skip context\" / \"fresh start\" / \"skip memory\" / [skip] for memory loading; Level 1 tasks skip completion verification.\n217: \n218: ---\n219: \n220: ### 🔒 POST-EXECUTION GATES\n221: \n222: #### MEMORY SAVE RULE [HARD] BLOCK\n223: Trigger: \"save context\", \"save memory\", `/memory:save`\n224: - If spec folder established at Gate 3 → USE IT (don't re-ask). Carry-over applies ONLY to memory saves\n225: - If NO folder and Gate 3 never answered → HARD BLOCK → Ask user\n226: - **Full save (DB + embeddings + graph):** `node .opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/scripts/dist/memory/generate-context.js`\n227:   - AI composes structured JSON with session context, writes to `/tmp/save-context-data.json`, passes as first arg. Alternatively use `--json '<inline-json>'` or `--stdin`.\n228:   - Also refreshes `graph-metadata.json` and `description.json` for the spec folder.\n229: - **Quick continuity update:** AI may directly edit `_memory.continuity` YAML frontmatter blocks in `implementation-summary.md` without running generate-context.js (per ADR-004). The resume ladder only reads continuity from `implementation-summary.md`.\n230: - **Memory mutation freshness:** Handlers that affect `memory_index` rows (`memory_save`, `memory_bulk_delete`) must invalidate the entity-density cache after commit so graph-channel routing sees fresh causal/entity state without waiting for the TTL.\n231: - **Indexing:** For immediate MCP visibility after save: `memory_index_scan({ specFolder })` or `memory_save()`\n232: - **Post-Save Review:** After `generate-context.js` completes, check the POST-SAVE QUALITY REVIEW output.\n233:   - **HIGH** issues: MUST manually patch via Edit tool (fix title, trigger_phrases, importance_tier)\n234:   - **MEDIUM** issues: patch when practical\n235:   - **PASSED/SKIPPED**: no action needed\n236: \n237: #### COMPLETION VERIFICATION RULE [HARD] BLOCK\n238: Trigger: Claiming \"done\", \"complete\", \"finished\", \"works\"\n239: 1. Run `bash .opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/scripts/spec/validate.sh <spec-folder> --strict` (Exit 0 = pass, 1 = warnings, 2 = errors).\n240: 2. Load `checklist.md` → verify ALL items → mark `[x]` with evidence.\n241: 3. Reconcile completion metadata: update `spec.md` Status, plan/checklist evidence, handover completion fields, and implementation-summary continuity so packet docs do not claim conflicting completion states.\n242: - Skip: Level 1 tasks (no checklist.md required).\n243: \n244: Completion metadata reconciliation covers:\n245: - `spec.md` status and shipped/current-state claims.\n246: - `plan.md` / `tasks.md` / `checklist.md` evidence rows.\n247: - `handover.md` or `_memory.continuity` fields when present.\n248: - `implementation-summary.md` final state, validation evidence, and continuation notes.\n249: \n250: #### VIOLATION RECOVERY [SELF-CORRECTION]\n251: Trigger: About to skip gates, or realized gates were skipped → STOP → STATE: \"Before I proceed, I need to ask about documentation:\" → ASK Gate 3 (A/B/C/D/E) → WAIT\n252: - **Exception:** If the user already answered Gate 3 earlier in this conversation for the same task, do NOT re-ask. Reuse the existing answer and proceed.\n253: \n254: #### Self-Check (before ANY tool-using response):\n255: - [ ] File modification? Asked spec folder question?\n256: - [ ] Skill routing verified?\n257: - [ ] Saving memory? Using `generate-context.js` (not Write tool)?\n258: - [ ] Aligned with ORIGINAL request? No scope drift?\n259: - [ ] Claiming completion? `checklist.md` verified?\n260: \n261: ---\n262: \n263: ## 3. 📝 SPEC FOLDER DOCUMENTATION\n264: \n265: Every conversation that modifies files MUST have a spec folder. **Full details:** system-spec-kit SKILL.md (§1 When to Use, §3 How it Works, §4 Rules)\n266: \n267: ### Documentation Levels\n268: \n269: | Level            | LOC                     | Required Files                                                         | Use When                                                                                          |\n270: | ---------------- | ----------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |\n271: | **1**            | <100                    | spec.md, plan.md, tasks.md, implementation-summary.md                  | All features (minimum)                                                                            |\n272: | **2**            | 100-499                 | Level 1 + checklist.md                                                 | QA validation needed                                                                              |\n273: | **3**            | ≥500                    | Level 2 + decision-record.md (+ optional research.md, resource-map.md) | Complex/architecture changes                                                                      |\n274: | **3+**           | Complexity 80+          | Level 3 + AI protocols, extended checklist, sign-offs                  | Multi-agent, enterprise governance                                                                |\n275: | **Phase Parent** | n/a (control file only) | spec.md, description.json, graph-metadata.json                         | Folder contains phase children (`[0-9]{3}-name/` subdirs with their own spec.md/description.json) |\n276: \n277: **Optional cross-cutting docs (any level)**: `handover.md`, `debug-delegation.md`, `research.md`, and `resource-map.md` - copy from `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/templates/` as needed. For phase parents that have undergone reorganization (renames, gap renumbering, consolidation), `context-index.md` provides a migration bridge — optional, no required template.\n278: \n279: **Phase Parent Mode:** When a spec folder contains at least one direct child matching `^[0-9]{3}-[a-z0-9-]+$` AND that child has `spec.md` OR `description.json`, the validator treats the folder as a phase parent and ONLY requires `{spec.md, description.json, graph-metadata.json}` at the parent level. Heavy docs (`plan.md`, `tasks.md`, `checklist.md`, `decision-record.md`, `implementation-summary.md`) live in the phase children where they stay accurate to that phase's actual work. Detection rule: `is_phase_parent()` (shell) and `isPhaseParent()` (TS/JS) are the single source of truth — both must agree. **Content discipline:** the phase-parent `spec.md` must NOT narrate consolidation, merge, or migration history — it documents root purpose, sub-phase control file, and what needs done. Migration history goes in `context-index.md` if needed. Resume on a phase parent first follows a fresh `derived.last_active_child_id` pointer from `graph-metadata.json`; missing, null, stale, or `--no-redirect` cases list child phases with statuses (per `/speckit:resume` step 3b) so the user can pick which phase to continue. Tolerant policy: legacy phase parents that retain heavy docs continue to validate; soft-deprecation is a follow-on packet.\n280: \n281: **Mandatory metadata:** Every spec folder (Level 1+) MUST contain `description.json` and `graph-metadata.json`. Both are auto-generated/refreshed by `generate-context.js` during canonical saves. `graph-metadata.json` stores lowercase derived status and falls back to `implementation-summary.md` presence plus checklist completion when explicit status is absent. If creating a spec folder manually or via template, run `generate-description.js` and the graph-metadata backfill to ensure both files exist. Spec folders without these files are invisible to memory search and graph traversal.\n282: \n283: **Rules:** When in doubt → higher level. LOC is soft guidance (risk/complexity can override). Single typo/whitespace fixes (<5 characters in one file) are exempt.\n284: \n285: **Spec folder path:** `.opencode/specs/[track]/[###-short-name]/` for tracked OpenCode packets, with phase children such as `[001-phase]/` under phase parents. Legacy/root `specs/[###-short-name]/` may exist, but current packet-local docs and metadata live under `.opencode/specs/`. | **Templates:** `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/templates/`\n286: \n287: ---\n288: \n289: ## 4. 🧑‍🏫 CONFIDENCE & CLARIFICATION FRAMEWORK\n290: \n291: #### Confidence Thresholds\n292: \n293: | Confidence   | Action                                       |\n294: | ------------ | -------------------------------------------- |\n295: | **≥80%**     | Proceed with citable source                  |\n296: | **40-79%**   | Proceed with caveats                         |\n297: | **<40%**     | Ask for clarification or mark \"UNKNOWN\"      |\n298: | **Override** | Blockers/conflicts → ask regardless of score |\n299: \n300: #### Logic-Sync Protocol\n301: \n302: On contradiction (Spec vs Code, conflicting requirements) → HALT → Report \"LOGIC-SYNC REQUIRED: [Fact A] contradicts [Fact B]\" → Ask \"Which truth prevails?\"\n303: \n304: #### Escalation\n305: \n306: Confidence stays <80% after two failed attempts → ask with 2-3 options. Blockers beyond control → escalate with evidence and proposed next step.\n307: \n308: ---\n309: \n310: ## 5. 🤖 AGENT ROUTING\n311: \n312: When using the orchestrate agent or Task tool for complex multi-step workflows, route to specialized agents:\n313: \n314: ### Runtime Agent Directory Resolution\n315: \n316: Use the agent directory that matches the active runtime/provider profile:\n317: \n318: | Runtime / Profile | Agent Directory     |\n319: | ----------------- | ------------------- |\n320: | **Opencode**      | `.opencode/agents/` |\n321: | **Claude Code**   | `.claude/agents/`   |\n322: | **Codex CLI**     | `.codex/agents/`    |\n323: | **Gemini CLI**    | `.gemini/agents/`   |\n324: \n325: **Resolution rule:** pick one directory by runtime and stay consistent for that workflow phase.\n326: \n327: ### Agent Definitions\n328: \n329: - **`@orchestrate`** - Multi-agent coordination, complex workflows\n330: - **`@code`** - Application-code implementation specialist (LEAF, write-capable). Stack-aware via `sk-code` skill delegation; fail-closed verification. Dispatched ONLY by `@orchestrate` (orchestrator-only convention).\n331: - **`@context`** - LEAF-only retrieval agent for codebase search, pattern discovery, and context loading. Uses memory triggers/context, memory search, CocoIndex, and direct code evidence. LEAF: no sub-agent dispatch, no Task tool, no writes.\n332: - **`@review`** - Code review, PRs, quality gates (READ-ONLY)\n333: - **`@debug`** - Fresh perspective debugging (5-phase root-cause). Dispatched via Task tool; retains exclusive write access for `debug-delegation.md`\n334: - **`@markdown`** - Template-first markdown/documentation executor (LEAF, write-capable). Handles `/create:*` commands, orchestrator-scoped spec-doc authoring, and any explicitly scoped markdown writing task with a resolved output path. Loads `sk-doc` on every invocation, reads the command-mapped or document-appropriate template before writing, and refuses only unscoped writes, path-ambiguous targets, or nested delegation. The Phase 0 gate is scope-based, not `/create:*`-only. Gate 3 still applies to writes unless the user or command contract has already supplied the answer.\n335: - **`@prompt-improver`** - Prompt engineering via `sk-prompt`. Dispatched by `/improve:prompt`\n336: - **`@ai-council`** - Deep AI Council planning architect for multi-seat deliberation, strategy comparison, critique, convergence, and packet-local `ai-council/**` artifacts.\n337: - **`@deep-research`** - Autonomous deep research iterations (LEAF). Dispatched by `/deep:start-research-loop`\n338: - **`@deep-review`** - Autonomous deep review iterations (LEAF, P0/P1/P2). Dispatched by `/deep:start-review-loop`\n339: - **`@deep-agent-improvement`** - Bounded agent improvement via `deep-agent-improvement`. Dispatched by `/improve:agent`\n340: \n341: #### Distributed Governance Rule\n342: \n343: - **Template + strict validate:** Any agent writing authored spec-folder docs (`spec.md`, `plan.md`, `tasks.md`, `checklist.md`, `implementation-summary.md`, `decision-record.md`, `handover.md`, `review-report.md`, `debug-delegation.md`, `resource-map.md`) MUST use templates from `.opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/templates/` and run `bash .opencode/skills/system-spec-kit/scripts/spec/validate.sh <spec-folder> --strict` after the write, before any completion claim.\n344: - **Continuity updates:** route through `/memory:save`.\n345: - **Deep-research exemption:** workflow-owned packet markdown (`research/iterations/*.md`, `research/deep-research-*.md`, progressive `research/research.md` updates) is exempt from the per-write strict-validate rule; `/deep:start-research-loop` instead runs targeted strict validation after every `spec.md` mutation it performs.\n346: - **Exclusive write access:** `@deep-research` owns `research/research.md`; `@debug` owns `debug-delegation.md`.\n347: \n348: ---\n349: \n350: ## 6. ⚙️  MCP TOOL ROUTING\n351: \n352: **Two systems:**\n353: \n354: 1. **Native MCP** (`opencode.json`) - Direct tools, called natively. **6 servers registered:**\n355:    - Sequential Thinking\n356:    - Spec Kit Memory (`mk-spec-memory`, 39 tools)\n357:    - Skill Advisor (`mk_skill_advisor`, 9 tools — 8 public + 1 internal)\n358:    - Code Graph (`mk_code_index`, 11 tools)\n359:    - CocoIndex Code\n360:    - Code Mode\n361: \n362: 2. **Code Mode MCP** (`.utcp_config.json`) - External tools via `call_tool_chain()`\n363:    - Figma, Github, ClickUp, Chrome DevTools, etc.\n364:    - Naming: `{manual_name}.{manual_name}_{tool_name}` (e.g., `clickup.clickup_get_teams({})`)\n365:    - Discovery: `search_tools()`, `list_tools()`, or read `.utcp_config.json`\n366:   \n367: ---\n368: \n369: ## 7. 🧩 SKILL ROUTING REFERENCE\n370: \n371: Skills are specialized, on-demand support that provide domain expertise.
